[21] thinking: **Evaluating material options**

I'm considering the choice between leather and coated fabric. The user mentioned a preference for a leather finish. I know that the IKEA products, like Grann/Bomstad in black, use top-grain leather with coated fabric possibly used elsewhere. The FRIHETEN model likely has a faux leather look, which may not satisfy the user’s criteria for genuine leather. To align with their request, I need to filter for options that specifically indicate a leather finish.

**Searching for budget-friendly options**

I'm looking for the most affordable sofas that meet the criteria of being black, having a leather finish, a rating of 4 or higher, and at least three seats. It seems like the KIVIK model for $1,149 and the FINNALA section sofa for $1,169 might be good options. However, I suspect the FRIHETEN Bomstad black sofa is made of coated fabric instead of genuine leather. I'll double-check the materials and make sure the choices fit the user's requirements.
